[30;1m29 | [0m[35m## changelog.yaml[0m
[30;1m30 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m31 | [0m[35mThe file must be named `changelog.yaml` and stored in the `changelogs/` subdirectory of the collecti[0m
[30;1m32 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m33 | [0m[35mAt the top level, there are two entries:[0m
[30;1m34 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m35 | [0m[35m1. A string `ancestor`, which can also be `null` or omitted if the changelog has no ancestor.[0m
[30;1m36 | [0m[35m2. A dictionary `releases`, which maps version numbers to release information.[0m
